**Summary**: Integration test for preemption from AC flavors.

## Description

#### What type of PR is this?

Adding tests, mostly to faithfully document the current Kueue behavior. \
So I guess this counts as:

/kind documentation

#### What this PR does / why we need it:

I'm adding a new integration test (parametrized, with numerous sub-cases), to document Kueue behavior around 2 recent issues related to preempting workloads which have been scheduled with an AdmissionCheck:

* For #5477, it documents that, although the `AdmissionChecks` in workload status may be in an undesired state temporarily, they ultimately get corrected by the Workload Controller.
* For #6966, it documents a surprising class of scenarios when preemption is stuck on HTTP request validation.

#### Which issue(s) this PR fixes:

For #5477, this PR may lead to closing it as WAI - or at least to decreasing its priority.

For #6966, this PR does not fix it - but it should help in diagnosing.

#### Special notes for your reviewer:

I have doubts about how this test should be ideally organized, and I'm open to feedback on this. \
The main points I'm not sure about:

1. Is it fine to have one test scenario packed with so many parameters, or should I be "more DAMP and less DRY"? \
   On one hand, I understand that too many `if`s in the test scenario can harm their readability. \
   OTOH, given that my test space already has `if`s on several independent dimensions (use RAM or not? expect success or deadlock? use AC on 1st flavor, or both, or none?) - applying "strict DAMP" would mean duplicating this test into _twelve_ separate `Describe` suites. (With more possibly to come if we invent other useful variations). This sounds like a maintenance nightmare. \
   Therefore, while I'm open for _some_ splitting and duplication, I've so far postponed it until it's actually requested in the review.

   To reduce the "deficit of DAMP" in these tests, I've tried hard to make each of the [test cases](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/6616deae5d3068e3171e48ce53d5ab3bd6c168b2/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1998-L2131) self-explaining, mostly by introducing helper names.

2. It's a bit unusual to have integration tests documenting _unintended behavior_ (which is the case for the `stuck` family here). \
   I believe this has a clear value: it not only shows things _don't go right_, it also shows _in detail how they go wrong_ (by explicit failure expectations: [1](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/6616deae5d3068e3171e48ce53d5ab3bd6c168b2/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1879-L1887), [2](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/6616deae5d3068e3171e48ce53d5ab3bd6c168b2/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1903-L1911), [3](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/6616deae5d3068e3171e48ce53d5ab3bd6c168b2/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1961-L1969), [4](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/6616deae5d3068e3171e48ce53d5ab3bd6c168b2/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1984-L1992)). \
   Yet, this also brings disadvantages, of at least 2 kinds:
   - general mental confusion ("test passed" now means "Kueue failed", and conversely);
   - possible prevention of improvement (imagine someone _accidentally_ fixes #6966 with their PR; then that PR will be technically _blocked_ by the proposed integration test, until someone realizes that the right thing to do is just to replace `stuck` with `works` as the "expected outcome").

   I've been thinking how to address this tradeoff best. \
   One option would be to insert the `stuck` cases but commented out. Though this would count as adding dead code, also feeling unhealthy. \
   So, my best idea is to have them uncommented, but with every expectation "which we'd actually _welcome to fail_" equipped with a comment explaining this - like e.g. [here](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/6616deae5d3068e3171e48ce53d5ab3bd6c168b2/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1907-L1909).

   Opinions on this are welcome.

3. Last, on the simple technical level, I'm not sure if this test still fits into `provisioning_test.go`, or should be rather placed in a separate file. (Or even folder?)


#### Does this PR introduce a user-facing change?

```release-note
NONE
```

```diff
 		// *** TEST CASES FOR https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5477 ***
 
-		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
-		testCase(works, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
+		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCPU),
```

  nit, instead of listing the calls could you change the structure to use testCases? This is much more idiomatic in golang, see: https://go.dev/wiki/TableDrivenTests
  
  Also, I think this is a bit too many integration tests, so while this is ok for experimentation we should reduce the number to only those capturing different execution paths.

  > nit, instead of listing the calls could you change the structure to use testCases? This is much more idiomatic in golang, see: https://go.dev/wiki/TableDrivenTests

  I can replace `testCase(...)` with `ginkgo.Entry(nil, ...)` everywhere if it helps.
  
  But is this what you meant?

```diff
@@ -1997,119 +1997,119 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.C
 		},

-		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
-		testCase(works, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
+		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCPU),
```

  Ah sorry, I didn't check carefully (leaving full review to @PBundyra ), so I didn't notice `testCase` is a wrapper around `ginkgo.Entry(nil, ...)`. 
  
  > I can replace testCase(...) with ginkgo.Entry(nil, ...) everywhere if it helps.
  
  Yes, I think I prefer to use this layer for two reasons:
  1. it is surprising as not broadly used in the codebase
  2. it does not supply the "description" for the entry. I think as we limit the number of test cases we should keep only those which bring functionally different scenarios, and describe each of them, emphasizing what is essential about them.

### Review by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) (commented) — 2025-09-26T15:53:28Z

- **test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go:2000** by [@tenzen-y](https://github.com/tenzen-y) — 2025-09-26T15:53:28Z
```diff
@@ -1997,119 +1997,119 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.C
 		},
 		// *** TEST CASES FOR https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5477 ***
 
-		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
-		testCase(works, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
+		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCPU),
```

  I have strong objections for `ginkgo.Entry` here.
  In case of webhook validation tests, table-driven cases could help us since the verifications are just executing CRUD objects w/o additional fat operations.
  
  However, such these proposed test cases, those have a lot of custom operations. 
  As you learned in contributor guide, the verbosity is respected rather than reusability in test.
  Thus, It should be better avoiding both `ginkgo.Entry` and `testCase`.
  
  Those should be implemented in BDD style.

### Review by [@olekzabl](https://github.com/olekzabl) (commented) — 2025-09-26T16:06:19Z

- **test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go:2000** by [@olekzabl](https://github.com/olekzabl) — 2025-09-26T16:06:19Z
```diff
@@ -1997,119 +1997,119 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.C
 		},
 		// *** TEST CASES FOR https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5477 ***
 
-		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
-		testCase(works, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
+		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCPU),
```

  Updates:
  
  * I reduced the number of test cases from 109 to 21. \
    I chose them to keep "the key points of the story". \
    I'm hoping this reduction is sufficient; otherwise I'd ask for some suggestions what else to cut out.
  
  * I replaced `testCase(...)` with `ginkgo.Entry(nil, ...)`. \
    I agree with point 1 of your rationale.
  
  * As for point 2:
  
    > it does not supply the "description" for the entry
  
    I did my best to supply this, by:
    * introducing a "sub-language of names" to get possibly clear param descriptions like
      ```
      (stuck, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCpu)
      ```
    * using a custom description generator ([here](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/518082aee7ee78757138e72a1723dec2fcea623a/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1991-L1993); also note the sub-stringers like [these](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/518082aee7ee78757138e72a1723dec2fcea623a/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1620-L1634))
    * leaving plenty of comments inside the list of cases to guide the reader through their role.
  
    If I was to specify a unique string description next to each test case, I think it'd clutter them more than help. \
    (But if reviewers disagree with that, I'll try to adhere :)

### Review by [@olekzabl](https://github.com/olekzabl) (commented) — 2025-09-26T16:30:43Z

- **test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go:2000** by [@olekzabl](https://github.com/olekzabl) — 2025-09-26T16:30:42Z
```diff
@@ -1997,119 +1997,119 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.C
 		},
 		// *** TEST CASES FOR https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5477 ***
 
-		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
-		testCase(works, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
+		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCPU),
```

  @tenzen-y 
  
  > Thus, It should be better avoiding both ginkgo.Entry and testCase.
  > Those should be implemented in BDD style.
  
  If I was to follow this entirely, then I think I'd need to give up one of the goals of this PR. Namely: to allow a systematic verification under which circumstances the issue #6966 hits and under which it doesn't.
  
  My findings so far is that #6966 hits under a conjunction of 3 conditions (in short: AC was used, RAM was requested, and the RAM config satisfies _some weird condition_ on the number of bytes). I was asked to send out an integration test verifying these claims. To achieve that goal, at the _very least_, I need the RAM request to be injectable as a parameter. (Because there, at least ~10 distinct values should be tested to reveal the picture).
  
  So, thinking of the "least DRY" way that could work here, it would be 5 or 6 separate suites, with **2** of them **still parametrized**:
  
  * Bare minimum:
    * `works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCPU` for both #5477 and #6966
    * `works, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCPU` for 5477
    * `works, noAC, memory("5G", "200M", defaultCPU)` for 6966
    * `works, firstFlavorAC, memory("5G", PARAM), defaultCPU` for 6966 - *parametrized* with a single string
    * `stuck, firstFlavorAC, memory("5G", PARAM), defaultCPU` for 6966 - *parametrized* with a single string
  * Nice to have:
    * `works, noAC, memory("5G", "200Mi"), cpu("3000", "2000")` for 6966 - to show that CPU divisible by 1000 is not problematic
  
  TBH I'm not very happy about that perspective - because if anyone comes in X weeks and asks another research question on #6966 (what if we introduce feature Y to the picture? what if we switch the value of Z to W? etc.) - it may lead to repeated work in several of those scenarios.
  
  But if this is agreed upon, I can refactor into this shape.
  
  WDYT?

### Review by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) (commented) — 2025-09-26T17:10:32Z

- **test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go:2000** by [@mimowo](https://github.com/mimowo) — 2025-09-26T17:10:32Z
```diff
@@ -1997,119 +1997,119 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.C
 		},
 		// *** TEST CASES FOR https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5477 ***
 
-		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
-		testCase(works, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
+		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCPU),
```

  My intuition tells me that matrix tests are great for experimentation and probing of the behavior to better understand the problem surface.However , when it comes to merging we should focus solely on the limited number of cases which trigger the unexpected behavior and describe them well. 
  
  Matrix tests without described intention will be hard to understand in the future, for example if they fail it will be unclear if for a good or bad reason.
  
  I will think about this more next week, but it may need to wait until 0.14 is out (Wednesday+) so that reviewers can get deeper into the issue faced.

### Review by [@olekzabl](https://github.com/olekzabl) (commented) — 2025-09-26T20:52:14Z

- **test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go:2000** by [@olekzabl](https://github.com/olekzabl) — 2025-09-26T20:52:14Z
```diff
@@ -1997,119 +1997,119 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.C
 		},
 		// *** TEST CASES FOR https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5477 ***
 
-		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
-		testCase(works, bothAC, noMemory, defaultCpu),
+		testCase(works, firstFlavorAC, noMemory, defaultCPU),
```

  > My intuition tells me that matrix tests are great for experimentation and probing of the behavior to better understand the problem surface.However , when it comes to merging we should focus solely on the limited number of cases which trigger the unexpected behavior and describe them well.
  
  This sounds good, as long as _merging_ indeed happens once _experimentation and probing_ is finished.
  
  * For #5477, this is applicable: we have just [2 relevant cases](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/518082aee7ee78757138e72a1723dec2fcea623a/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1996-L1997) which I can split & de-parametrize.
  
  * For #6966, it's less clear.
  
    I'm not sure if "experimentation and probing" has already finished here. \
    While I can reduce this PR e.g. to just 1 test case for undesired behavior, I'm not sure if there won't be a need to revert this reduction later on (at least locally, for experimenting again).
  
    For the good, I _have sent_ out this PR in its full shape. Hence, its original state has been "officially snapshotted" in Git history, moreover, with all my test cases passing (e.g. [here](https://prow.k8s.io/view/gs/kubernetes-ci-logs/pr-logs/pull/kubernetes-sigs_kueue/7010/pull-kueue-test-integration-baseline-main/1971563156492783616)). \
    Now, anyone can pull & continue investigating from there, if there's a need. \
    (Up to a threat of getting outdated, but it's still a win). \
    So _now_ I'm more willing to reduce this PR than when I was _sending_ it.
  
    And then, in fact, even retaining just 1 `stuck` case is unhealthy in some way. \
    It'd be an integration test documenting an _undesired_ behavior, which I'm still not sure how to deal best with. (See point 2 of my initial comment on this PR).
  
  So - maybe _now_ the best approach is to leave only [these 2 cases](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/518082aee7ee78757138e72a1723dec2fcea623a/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go#L1996-L1997) (split to 2 independent scenarios), and give up merging any evidence for #6966?

- **test/integration/singlecluster/controller/admissionchecks/provisioning/provisioning_test.go:1625** by [@PBundyra](https://github.com/PBundyra) — 2025-10-02T14:24:36Z
```diff
@@ -1511,3 +1513,431 @@ var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.ContinueOnFailure
 		})
 	})
 })
+
+var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.ContinueOnFailure, func() {
+	var (
+		ns             *corev1.Namespace
+		wlKey          types.NamespacedName
+		wl2Key         types.NamespacedName
+		ac1            *kueue.AdmissionCheck
+		ac2            *kueue.AdmissionCheck
+		prc            *kueue.ProvisioningRequestConfig
+		provReqKey     types.NamespacedName
+		provReqKey2    types.NamespacedName
+		rf1            *kueue.ResourceFlavor
+		rf2            *kueue.ResourceFlavor
+		cq             *kueue.ClusterQueue
+		lq             *kueue.LocalQueue
+		createdRequest autoscaling.ProvisioningRequest
+		priorityClass  *kueue.WorkloadPriorityClass
+		wlObj          kueue.Workload
+	)
+
+	const (
+		flavor1Name       = "flavor-1"
+		flavor2Name       = "flavor-2"
+		flavor1Ref        = kueue.ResourceFlavorReference(flavor1Name)
+		flavor2Ref        = kueue.ResourceFlavorReference(flavor2Name)
+		priorityClassName = "priority-class"
+		priorityValue     = 1000
+	)
+
+	baseConfig := testing.MakeProvisioningRequestConfig("prov-config").ProvisioningClass("provisioning-class")
+
+	ginkgo.JustBeforeEach(func() {
+		fwk.StartManager(ctx, cfg, managerSetup(runScheduler, runJobController))
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.JustBeforeEach(func() {
+		ns = util.CreateNamespaceFromPrefixWithLog(ctx, k8sClient, "provisioning-")
+
+		rf1 = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(flavor1Name).NodeLabel("ns1", "ns1v").Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, rf1)
+		rf2 = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(flavor2Name).NodeLabel("ns2", "ns2v").Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, rf2)
+
+		priorityClass = testing.MakeWorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).PriorityValue(priorityValue).Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, priorityClass)
+
+		prc = baseConfig.Clone().RetryLimit(1).Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, prc)
+
+		ac1 = testing.MakeAdmissionCheck("ac-prov").
+			ControllerName(kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName).
+			Parameters(kueue.GroupVersion.Group, "ProvisioningRequestConfig", "prov-config").
+			Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, ac1)
+
+		ac2 = testing.MakeAdmissionCheck("ac-prov2").
+			ControllerName(kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName).
+			Parameters(kueue.GroupVersion.Group, "ProvisioningRequestConfig", "prov-config").
+			Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, ac2)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, cq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, lq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, priorityClass, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, prc, true)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		fwk.StopManager(ctx)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.When("A workload is preempted from a flavor which uses an admission check", func() {
+		ginkgo.It("Should be successfully re-admitted on another flavor without an admission check", func() {
+			ginkgo.By("Set up ClusterQueue and LocalQueue", func() {
+				cq = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+					Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+						WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+					}).
+					ResourceGroup(
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf1.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.75").Obj(),
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf2.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.5").Obj(),
+					).
+					AdmissionCheckStrategy(kueue.AdmissionCheckStrategyRule{
+						Name:      kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name),
+						OnFlavors: []kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{flavor1Ref},
+					}).
+					Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+				util.ExpectClusterQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+
+				lq = testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(cq.Name).Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+				util.ExpectLocalQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit the Job", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "500m")
```

  Let's stick with Workloads only, there is no need to introduce another layer (Jobs) in integration tests

```diff
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, ac1)
+

+			ControllerName(kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName).
+			Parameters(kueue.GroupVersion.Group, "ProvisioningRequestConfig", "prov-config").

+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, ac2)

+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, cq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, lq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, priorityClass, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, prc, true)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		fwk.StopManager(ctx)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.When("A workload is preempted from a flavor which uses an admission check", func() {
+		ginkgo.It("Should be successfully re-admitted on another flavor without an admission check", func() {
+			ginkgo.By("Set up ClusterQueue and LocalQueue", func() {
+				cq = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+					Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+						WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+					}).
+					ResourceGroup(
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf1.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.75").Obj(),
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf2.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.5").Obj(),
+					).
+					AdmissionCheckStrategy(kueue.AdmissionCheckStrategyRule{

+						OnFlavors: []kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{flavor1Ref},
+					}).
+					Obj()

+				util.ExpectClusterQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, cq)

+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+				util.ExpectLocalQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit the Job", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "500m")
+				job1 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job1)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job1, true)
+				})
+				wlKey = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job1.Name, job1.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have QuotaReserved", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusQuotaReserved))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 to be created", func() {
+				provReqKey = types.NamespacedName{
+					Namespace: wlKey.Namespace,
+					Name:      provisioning.ProvisioningRequestName(wlKey.Name, kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name), 1),
+				}
+
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("set the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 as Provisioned", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					apimeta.SetStatusCondition(&createdRequest.Status.Conditions, metav1.Condition{
+						Type:   autoscaling.Provisioned,
+						Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+						Reason: autoscaling.Provisioned,
+					})
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor1Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit a high-priority job2", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					WorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "750m")
+				job2 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job2)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job2, true)
+				})
+				wl2Key = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job2.Name, job2.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to have QuotaReserved or be Admitted", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.BeElementOf(
+						workload.StatusQuotaReserved,
+						workload.StatusAdmitted,
+					))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be no longer Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
```

  ```suggestion
  			ginkgo.By("await for the wl1 to be no longer Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
  ```

```diff
+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, cq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, lq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, priorityClass, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, prc, true)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		fwk.StopManager(ctx)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.When("A workload is preempted from a flavor which uses an admission check", func() {
+		ginkgo.It("Should be successfully re-admitted on another flavor without an admission check", func() {
+			ginkgo.By("Set up ClusterQueue and LocalQueue", func() {
+				cq = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+					Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+						WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+					}).
+					ResourceGroup(
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf1.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.75").Obj(),
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf2.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.5").Obj(),
+					).
+					AdmissionCheckStrategy(kueue.AdmissionCheckStrategyRule{
+						Name:      kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name),
+						OnFlavors: []kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{flavor1Ref},
+					}).
+					Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+				util.ExpectClusterQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+
+				lq = testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(cq.Name).Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+				util.ExpectLocalQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit the Job", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "500m")
+				job1 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job1)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job1, true)
+				})
+				wlKey = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job1.Name, job1.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have QuotaReserved", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusQuotaReserved))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 to be created", func() {
+				provReqKey = types.NamespacedName{
+					Namespace: wlKey.Namespace,
+					Name:      provisioning.ProvisioningRequestName(wlKey.Name, kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name), 1),
+				}
+
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("set the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 as Provisioned", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					apimeta.SetStatusCondition(&createdRequest.Status.Conditions, metav1.Condition{
+						Type:   autoscaling.Provisioned,
+						Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+						Reason: autoscaling.Provisioned,
+					})
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor1Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit a high-priority job2", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					WorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "750m")
+				job2 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job2)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job2, true)
+				})
+				wl2Key = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job2.Name, job2.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to have QuotaReserved or be Admitted", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.BeElementOf(
+						workload.StatusQuotaReserved,
+						workload.StatusAdmitted,
+					))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be no longer Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+					var isAdmittedOnFlavor1 = false
+					if wlObj.Status.Admission != nil {
+						psa := wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments
+						isAdmittedOnFlavor1 = len(psa) == 1 &&
+							psa[0].Flavors[corev1.ResourceCPU] == flavor1Ref
+					}
+
+					g.Expect(isAdmittedOnFlavor1).To(gomega.BeFalse())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-2", func() {
```

```diff
+
```

```diff
+				provReqKey = types.NamespacedName{
+					Namespace: wlKey.Namespace,
+					Name:      provisioning.ProvisioningRequestName(wlKey.Name, kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name), 1),
+				}
+
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("set the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 as Provisioned", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					apimeta.SetStatusCondition(&createdRequest.Status.Conditions, metav1.Condition{
+						Type:   autoscaling.Provisioned,
+						Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+						Reason: autoscaling.Provisioned,
+					})
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor1Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit a high-priority job2", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					WorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "750m")
+				job2 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job2)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job2, true)
+				})
+				wl2Key = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job2.Name, job2.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to have QuotaReserved or be Admitted", func() {
```

  Let's avoid using OR here, I think the wl2 should have just QuotaReserved here on flavor-1, as it would be Admitted only after ProvisioningRequest was set to `Provisioned`

```diff
+var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.ContinueOnFailure, func() {
+	var (
+		ns             *corev1.Namespace
+		wlKey          types.NamespacedName
+		wl2Key         types.NamespacedName
+		ac1            *kueue.AdmissionCheck
+		ac2            *kueue.AdmissionCheck

+		rf2            *kueue.ResourceFlavor

+		lq             *kueue.LocalQueue

+	)
+

+		flavor1Name       = "flavor-1"
+		flavor2Name       = "flavor-2"
+		flavor1Ref        = kueue.ResourceFlavorReference(flavor1Name)
+		flavor2Ref        = kueue.ResourceFlavorReference(flavor2Name)
+		priorityClassName = "priority-class"
+		priorityValue     = 1000
+	)
+
+	baseConfig := testing.MakeProvisioningRequestConfig("prov-config").ProvisioningClass("provisioning-class")
+

+		fwk.StartManager(ctx, cfg, managerSetup(runScheduler, runJobController))
+	})
+

+		ns = util.CreateNamespaceFromPrefixWithLog(ctx, k8sClient, "provisioning-")
+
+		rf1 = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(flavor1Name).NodeLabel("ns1", "ns1v").Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, rf1)
+		rf2 = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(flavor2Name).NodeLabel("ns2", "ns2v").Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, rf2)
+
+		priorityClass = testing.MakeWorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).PriorityValue(priorityValue).Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, priorityClass)
+
+		prc = baseConfig.Clone().RetryLimit(1).Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, prc)
+
+		ac1 = testing.MakeAdmissionCheck("ac-prov").
+			ControllerName(kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName).
+			Parameters(kueue.GroupVersion.Group, "ProvisioningRequestConfig", "prov-config").
+			Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, ac1)
+
+		ac2 = testing.MakeAdmissionCheck("ac-prov2").
+			ControllerName(kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName).
+			Parameters(kueue.GroupVersion.Group, "ProvisioningRequestConfig", "prov-config").
+			Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, ac2)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, cq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, lq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, priorityClass, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, prc, true)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		fwk.StopManager(ctx)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.When("A workload is preempted from a flavor which uses an admission check", func() {
+		ginkgo.It("Should be successfully re-admitted on another flavor without an admission check", func() {
+			ginkgo.By("Set up ClusterQueue and LocalQueue", func() {
+				cq = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+					Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+						WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+					}).
+					ResourceGroup(
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf1.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.75").Obj(),
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf2.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.5").Obj(),
+					).
+					AdmissionCheckStrategy(kueue.AdmissionCheckStrategyRule{
+						Name:      kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name),
+						OnFlavors: []kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{flavor1Ref},
+					}).
+					Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+				util.ExpectClusterQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+
+				lq = testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(cq.Name).Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+				util.ExpectLocalQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit the Job", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "500m")
+				job1 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job1)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job1, true)
+				})
+				wlKey = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job1.Name, job1.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have QuotaReserved", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusQuotaReserved))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})

+			ginkgo.By("await for the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 to be created", func() {

+				}
+
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("set the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 as Provisioned", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					apimeta.SetStatusCondition(&createdRequest.Status.Conditions, metav1.Condition{
+						Type:   autoscaling.Provisioned,
+						Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+						Reason: autoscaling.Provisioned,
+					})
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor1Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit a high-priority job2", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					WorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "750m")
+				job2 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job2)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job2, true)
+				})
+				wl2Key = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job2.Name, job2.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to have QuotaReserved or be Admitted", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.BeElementOf(
+						workload.StatusQuotaReserved,
+						workload.StatusAdmitted,
+					))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be no longer Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+					var isAdmittedOnFlavor1 = false
+					if wlObj.Status.Admission != nil {
+						psa := wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments
+						isAdmittedOnFlavor1 = len(psa) == 1 &&
+							psa[0].Flavors[corev1.ResourceCPU] == flavor1Ref
+					}
+
+					g.Expect(isAdmittedOnFlavor1).To(gomega.BeFalse())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-2", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor2Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have status for AdmissionCheck1 cleared", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					hasAc1 := false
+					for _, ac := range wlObj.Status.AdmissionChecks {
+						if ac.Name == kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name) {
+							hasAc1 = true
+							break
+						}
+					}
+					g.Expect(hasAc1).Should(gomega.BeFalse())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+		})
+

+

+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+				util.ExpectLocalQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit the Job", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "500m")
+				job1 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job1)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job1, true)
+				})
```

```diff
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusQuotaReserved))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 to be created", func() {
+				provReqKey = types.NamespacedName{
+					Namespace: wlKey.Namespace,
+					Name:      provisioning.ProvisioningRequestName(wlKey.Name, kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name), 1),
+				}
+
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("set the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 as Provisioned", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					apimeta.SetStatusCondition(&createdRequest.Status.Conditions, metav1.Condition{
+						Type:   autoscaling.Provisioned,
+						Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+						Reason: autoscaling.Provisioned,
+					})
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor1Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit a high-priority job2", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					WorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "750m")
+				job2 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job2)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job2, true)
+				})
+				wl2Key = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job2.Name, job2.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to have QuotaReserved or be Admitted", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.BeElementOf(
+						workload.StatusQuotaReserved,
+						workload.StatusAdmitted,
+					))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be no longer Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+					var isAdmittedOnFlavor1 = false
+					if wlObj.Status.Admission != nil {
+						psa := wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments
+						isAdmittedOnFlavor1 = len(psa) == 1 &&
+							psa[0].Flavors[corev1.ResourceCPU] == flavor1Ref
+					}
+
+					g.Expect(isAdmittedOnFlavor1).To(gomega.BeFalse())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-2", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor2Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have status for AdmissionCheck1 cleared", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					hasAc1 := false
+					for _, ac := range wlObj.Status.AdmissionChecks {
+						if ac.Name == kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name) {
+							hasAc1 = true
+							break
+						}
+					}
+					g.Expect(hasAc1).Should(gomega.BeFalse())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+		})
+
+		ginkgo.It("Should be successfully re-admitted on another flavor with another admission check", func() {

+					Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+						WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+					}).
+					ResourceGroup(

+					).
+					AdmissionCheckStrategy(
+						kueue.AdmissionCheckStrategyRule{
+							Name:      kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name),
+							OnFlavors: []kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{flavor1Ref},
+						},
+						kueue.AdmissionCheckStrategyRule{
+							Name:      kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac2.Name),
+							OnFlavors: []kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{flavor2Ref},
+						},
+					).
+					Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+				util.ExpectClusterQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+
+				lq = testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(cq.Name).Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+				util.ExpectLocalQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit the Job", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "500m")
+				job1 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job1)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job1, true)
+				})

+			})

+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be created", func() {

+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have QuotaReserved", func() {
```

```diff
@@ -67,8 +71,40 @@ var _ = ginkgo.AfterSuite(func() {
 	fwk.Teardown()
 })
 
-func managerSetup() framework.ManagerSetup {
+type managerSetupOpts struct {
+	runScheduler     bool
+	runJobController bool
+}
+
+type managerSetupOption func(*managerSetupOpts)
+
+func runScheduler(opts *managerSetupOpts) {
+	opts.runScheduler = true
+}
+
+func runJobController(opts *managerSetupOpts) {
+	opts.runJobController = true
+}
+
+func managerSetup(options ...managerSetupOption) framework.ManagerSetup {
 	return func(ctx context.Context, mgr manager.Manager) {
+		var opts managerSetupOpts
+		for _, opt := range options {
+			opt(&opts)
+		}
+
+		var jobReconciler jobframework.JobReconcilerInterface
+
+		if opts.runJobController {
+			var err error
+			jobReconciler, err = job.NewReconciler(
+				ctx,
+				mgr.GetClient(),
+				mgr.GetFieldIndexer(),
+				mgr.GetEventRecorderFor(constants.JobControllerName))
+			gomega.Expect(err).NotTo(gomega.HaveOccurred())
+		}
```

  Yeah, originally I was thinking about the potential interaction with this code: https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/main/pkg/controller/jobframework/reconciler.go#L536-L544
  
  However, looking at the code it does not interact with the status.admissionChecks. 
  
  I'm ok with both approaches as both have some merit:
  - Job controller + scheduler + workload controller + prov req test the entire flow making sure there are not "unexpected" players
  - as we now understand thanks to the [excellent summary](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/issues/5477#issuecomment-3330929574) that there is no issue thanks to workload_controller, but that was far from obvious at the beginning
  
  No strong view.

```diff
 })
+
+var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.ContinueOnFailure, func() {
```

  Actually, it is ok to keep the interaction with Scheduler in the dedicated Describe. This is what we are doing for example [here](https://github.com/kubernetes-sigs/kueue/blob/40303177236412336043357d735493abfdb974c7/test/integration/singlecluster/controller/jobs/pytorchjob/pytorchjob_controller_test.go#L444). I think it improves readability, the trade-off with running time is not clear to me.

```diff
+var _ = ginkgo.Describe("Provisioning with scheduling", ginkgo.Ordered, ginkgo.ContinueOnFailure, func() {
+	var (
+		ns             *corev1.Namespace
+		wlKey          types.NamespacedName
+		wl2Key         types.NamespacedName

+		ac2            *kueue.AdmissionCheck

+		flavor1Name       = "flavor-1"
+		flavor2Name       = "flavor-2"
+		flavor1Ref        = kueue.ResourceFlavorReference(flavor1Name)
+		flavor2Ref        = kueue.ResourceFlavorReference(flavor2Name)
+		priorityClassName = "priority-class"
+		priorityValue     = 1000
+	)
+
+	baseConfig := testing.MakeProvisioningRequestConfig("prov-config").ProvisioningClass("provisioning-class")
+
+	ginkgo.JustBeforeEach(func() {
+		fwk.StartManager(ctx, cfg, managerSetup(runScheduler, runJobController))
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.JustBeforeEach(func() {
+		ns = util.CreateNamespaceFromPrefixWithLog(ctx, k8sClient, "provisioning-")
+
+		rf1 = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(flavor1Name).NodeLabel("ns1", "ns1v").Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, rf1)
+		rf2 = testing.MakeResourceFlavor(flavor2Name).NodeLabel("ns2", "ns2v").Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, rf2)
+
+		priorityClass = testing.MakeWorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).PriorityValue(priorityValue).Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, priorityClass)
+
+		prc = baseConfig.Clone().RetryLimit(1).Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, prc)
+
+		ac1 = testing.MakeAdmissionCheck("ac-prov").
+			ControllerName(kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName).
+			Parameters(kueue.GroupVersion.Group, "ProvisioningRequestConfig", "prov-config").
+			Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, ac1)
+
+		ac2 = testing.MakeAdmissionCheck("ac-prov2").
+			ControllerName(kueue.ProvisioningRequestControllerName).
+			Parameters(kueue.GroupVersion.Group, "ProvisioningRequestConfig", "prov-config").
+			Obj()
+		util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, ac2)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		gomega.Expect(util.DeleteNamespace(ctx, k8sClient, ns)).To(gomega.Succeed())
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, cq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, lq, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, rf2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, priorityClass, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac1, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, ac2, true)
+		util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, prc, true)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.AfterEach(func() {
+		fwk.StopManager(ctx)
+	})
+
+	ginkgo.When("A workload is preempted from a flavor which uses an admission check", func() {
+		ginkgo.It("Should be successfully re-admitted on another flavor without an admission check", func() {
+			ginkgo.By("Set up ClusterQueue and LocalQueue", func() {
+				cq = testing.MakeClusterQueue("cluster-queue").
+					Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+						WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+					}).
+					ResourceGroup(
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf1.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.75").Obj(),
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf2.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.5").Obj(),
+					).
+					AdmissionCheckStrategy(kueue.AdmissionCheckStrategyRule{
+						Name:      kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name),
+						OnFlavors: []kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{flavor1Ref},
+					}).
+					Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+				util.ExpectClusterQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+
+				lq = testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(cq.Name).Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+				util.ExpectLocalQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit the Job", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "500m")
+				job1 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job1)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job1, true)
+				})
+				wlKey = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job1.Name, job1.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have QuotaReserved", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusQuotaReserved))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 to be created", func() {
+				provReqKey = types.NamespacedName{
+					Namespace: wlKey.Namespace,
+					Name:      provisioning.ProvisioningRequestName(wlKey.Name, kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name), 1),
+				}
+
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("set the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 as Provisioned", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					apimeta.SetStatusCondition(&createdRequest.Status.Conditions, metav1.Condition{
+						Type:   autoscaling.Provisioned,
+						Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+						Reason: autoscaling.Provisioned,
+					})
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor1Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
```

  nit, I would inline that.
  
  Also, `Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments` is already set on quota reservation, so I would prefer checking it there, so that it is early established we are using flavor-1. Here we can just check workload.IsAdmitted I think.

```diff
+					Preemption(kueue.ClusterQueuePreemption{
+						WithinClusterQueue: kueue.PreemptionPolicyLowerPriority,
+					}).
+					ResourceGroup(
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf1.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.75").Obj(),
+						*testing.MakeFlavorQuotas(rf2.Name).Resource(corev1.ResourceCPU, "0.5").Obj(),
+					).
+					AdmissionCheckStrategy(kueue.AdmissionCheckStrategyRule{
+						Name:      kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name),
+						OnFlavors: []kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{flavor1Ref},
+					}).
+					Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+				util.ExpectClusterQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, cq)
+
+				lq = testing.MakeLocalQueue("queue", ns.Name).ClusterQueue(cq.Name).Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+				util.ExpectLocalQueuesToBeActive(ctx, k8sClient, lq)
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit the Job", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job1", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "500m")
+				job1 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job1)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job1, true)
+				})
+				wlKey = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job1.Name, job1.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have QuotaReserved", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusQuotaReserved))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 to be created", func() {
+				provReqKey = types.NamespacedName{
+					Namespace: wlKey.Namespace,
+					Name:      provisioning.ProvisioningRequestName(wlKey.Name, kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name), 1),
+				}
+
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("set the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 as Provisioned", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					apimeta.SetStatusCondition(&createdRequest.Status.Conditions, metav1.Condition{
+						Type:   autoscaling.Provisioned,
+						Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+						Reason: autoscaling.Provisioned,
+					})
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor1Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("submit a high-priority job2", func() {
+				jobBuilder := testingjob.MakeJob("job2", ns.Name).
+					Queue(kueue.LocalQueueName(lq.Name)).
+					WorkloadPriorityClass(priorityClassName).
+					Request(corev1.ResourceCPU, "750m")
+				job2 := jobBuilder.Obj()
+				util.MustCreate(ctx, k8sClient, job2)
+				ginkgo.DeferCleanup(func() {
+					util.ExpectObjectToBeDeleted(ctx, k8sClient, job2, true)
+				})
+				wl2Key = types.NamespacedName{Name: workloadjob.GetWorkloadNameForJob(job2.Name, job2.UID), Namespace: ns.Name}
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to be created", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for wl2 to have QuotaReserved or be Admitted", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wl2Key, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.BeElementOf(
+						workload.StatusQuotaReserved,
+						workload.StatusAdmitted,
+					))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be no longer Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+
+					var isAdmittedOnFlavor1 = false
+					if wlObj.Status.Admission != nil {
+						psa := wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments
+						isAdmittedOnFlavor1 = len(psa) == 1 &&
+							psa[0].Flavors[corev1.ResourceCPU] == flavor1Ref
+					}
+
+					g.Expect(isAdmittedOnFlavor1).To(gomega.BeFalse())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-2", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor2Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to have status for AdmissionCheck1 cleared", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					hasAc1 := false
+					for _, ac := range wlObj.Status.AdmissionChecks {
+						if ac.Name == kueue.AdmissionCheckReference(ac1.Name) {
+							hasAc1 = true
+							break
+						}
+					}
+					g.Expect(hasAc1).Should(gomega.BeFalse())
```

  Let's use some helper for that, maybe `admissioncheck.FindAdmissionCheck` and verfiy nil returned, or some gomega helper.

```diff
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("set the ProvisioningRequest on flavor-1 as Provisioned", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, provReqKey, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					apimeta.SetStatusCondition(&createdRequest.Status.Conditions, metav1.Condition{
+						Type:   autoscaling.Provisioned,
+						Status: metav1.ConditionTrue,
+						Reason: autoscaling.Provisioned,
+					})
+					g.Expect(k8sClient.Status().Update(ctx, &createdRequest)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+				}, util.Timeout, util.Interval).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+			})
+
+			ginkgo.By("await for the Workload to be Admitted on flavor-1", func() {
+				gomega.Eventually(func(g gomega.Gomega) {
+					gomega.Expect(k8sClient.Get(ctx, wlKey, &wlObj)).Should(gomega.Succeed())
+					g.Expect(workload.Status(&wlObj)).To(gomega.Equal(workload.StatusAdmitted))
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments).Should(gomega.HaveLen(1))
+
+					var expectedFlavors = map[corev1.ResourceName]kueue.ResourceFlavorReference{
+						corev1.ResourceCPU: flavor1Ref,
+					}
+					g.Expect(wlObj.Status.Admission.PodSetAssignments[0].Flavors).To(gomega.Equal(expectedFlavors))
```
